# 管控自定义分类

## 每次进入页面时检查，查询自定义分类表是否存在数据

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexCustomClassify/controller/ICustomClassifyServiceController/checkGroup?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomClassifyServiceController.checkGroup

方法参数：(无)

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json
(无)
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "false",	//存在数据返回true，不存在数据返回false
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 如果不存在数据，提示选择导入短编码，则初始化自定义分类表

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexCustomClassify/controller/ICustomClassifyServiceController/createCustomClassify?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomClassifyServiceController.createCustomClassify

方法参数：HashMap<String, Object> paraMap

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "modifier":"ht"	//登录用户名
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "true",	//添加数据成功返回true，失败返回false
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 如果短编码存在，则继续初始化自定义分类关联表

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexCustomClassify/controller/ICustomClassifyServiceController/exportShortNum?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomClassifyServiceController.exportShortNum

方法参数：HashMap<String, Object> paraMap

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json
{
    “modifier”:"ht"
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "true",	//添加数据成功返回true，失败返回false
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## A区-查询自定义分类

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexCustomClassify/controller/ICustomClassifyServiceController/getCustomClassifyA?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomClassifyServiceController.getCustomClassifyA

方法参数：HashMap<String, Object> paraMap

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json
{}	//传的是空map
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "dataList": [
            {
                "id": "133",	//唯一id
                "modifier": "",	//修改人
                "startUseDate": "2021-01-16 13:26:49",
                "endUseDate": "2021-01-16 13:26:49",
                "auditState": 1,	//审核状态
                "operator": "",	//审核人
                "c_GROUP_CODE": "123123",	//分类代码
                "c_GROUP_NAME": "1231312"	//分类名称
            }
        ],
        "headKeyList": [
            {
                "key": "C_GROUP_CODE",
                "text": "分类代码",
                "align": "L",
                "serviceId": "",
                "showName": "",
                "isShow": "",
                "width": "",
                "sortable": "",
                "order": "",
                "isExport": "",
                "isFrozen": "",
                "typeCode": "",
                "defaultDictTypeValue": "",
                "dictType": ""
            },
            {
                "key": "C_GROUP_NAME",
                "text": "分类名称",
                "align": "L",
                "serviceId": "",
                "showName": "",
                "isShow": "",
                "width": "",
                "sortable": "",
                "order": "",
                "isExport": "",
                "isFrozen": "",
                "typeCode": "",
                "defaultDictTypeValue": "",
                "dictType": ""
            }
        ],
        "showConvertAssemble": {},
        "page": {
            "pageCount": 0,
            "currPage": 1,
            "pageSize": 100,
            "totalNum": 0,
            "usePage": true
        },
        "operRes": "Success",
        "listDataClass": "CustomClassify",
        "menuId": "monitorCustomClassifyA",
        "retValue": ""
    },
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## A区-删除自定义分类

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexCustomClassify/controller/ICustomClassifyServiceController/deleteById/list?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomClassifyServiceController.deleteById

方法参数：List\<BasePojo> pojoList

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json
[
    {
        "c_GROUP_CODE":"shortnum",	//分类代码
        "c_GROUP_NAME":"shortnum",	//分类名称
        "auditState":0,
        "operator":"",
        "auditDate":null,
        "modifier":"ht",
        "modifyDate":null,
        "id":"292"
    }
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000002\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":\"monitorCustomClassifyA\",\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{},\"cidenList\":[]}}",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## A区-审核自定义分类

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexCustomClassify/controller/ICustomClassifyServiceController/auditById/list?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomClassifyServiceController.auditById

方法参数：List\<BasePojo> pojoList

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json
[
    {
        "c_GROUP_CODE":"shortnum",	//分类代码
        "c_GROUP_NAME":"shortnum",	//分类名称
        "auditState":0,
        "operator":"",
        "auditDate":null,
        "modifier":"ht",
        "modifyDate":null,
        "id":"292"
    }
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000003\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":\"monitorCustomClassifyA\",\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{},\"cidenList\":[\"292\"]}}",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```

方法名：ICustomClassifyServiceController.unAuditById

```json
    {
        "c_GROUP_CODE":"shortnum",	//分类代码
        "c_GROUP_NAME":"shortnum",	//分类名称

        "operator":"",
        "auditDate":null,
```

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomClassifyServiceController.updateById

方法参数：List\<BasePojo> pojoList

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json
[
    {
        "c_GROUP_CODE":"shortnum",	//分类代码
        "c_GROUP_NAME":"shortnum",	//分类名称
        "auditState":0,
        "operator":"",
        "auditDate":null,
        "modifier":"ht",
        "modifyDate":null,
        "id":"292"
    }
]
```

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000006\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":\"monitorCustomClassifyA\",\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{},\"cidenList\":[]}}",
    "message": "",
```

## A区-新增自定义分类

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexCustomClassify/controller/ICustomClassifyServiceController/insert/list?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomClassifyServiceController.insert

方法参数：List\<BasePojo> pojoList

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json
[
    {
        "c_GROUP_CODE":"001",
        "c_GROUP_NAME":"001",
        "auditState":0,
        "operator":"",
        "auditDate":null,
        "modifier":"ht",
        "modifyDate":null,
        "id":""
    }
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000001\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":\"monitorCustomClassifyA\",\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{\"aa\":\"1\",\"bb\":\"2\"},\"cidenList\":[\"299\"]}}",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## B区-查询自定义分类关联组合信息

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexCustomClassify/controller/ICustomGroupRelaDataServiceController/queryByCondition/page?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomGroupRelaDataServiceController.queryByCondition

方法参数：RestfulQueryConditionVo restfulQueryConditionVo

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "paraMap":{
        "C_GROUP_CODE":"shortnum",	//分类代码
        "C_GROUP_NAME":"shortnum",	//分类名称
        "PORT_CODES":"3rt4234|1t2222",	//组合代码，多个|分隔
        "LEVEL":"UNIT_LAYER,PORT_LAYER",	//组合层级，多个逗号分隔，单元层：UNIT_LAYER，组合层：PORT_LAYER，所有层：2个用逗号分隔
        "dataClass":"CustomGroupRelaData",	//数据pojo，写死
        "N_CHECK_STATE":"SearchAll"	//审核状态，SearchAll：所有，SearchAudit：已审核，SearchUnAudit：未审核
    },
    "page":{	//分页信息
        "currPage":1,	//当前页
        "pageCount":0,	//总页数
        "totalNum":1,	//总记录数
        "pageSize":100,	//当前页记录数
        "usePage":true	//是否使用分页
    }
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "dataList": [
            {
                "id": "25814",
                "modifier": "ht",
                "modifyDate": "20210207 17:53:58",
                "startUseDate": "2021-02-08 14:01:32",
                "endUseDate": "2021-02-08 14:01:32",
                "auditState": 0,	//审核状态
                "operator": "",

                "c_PORT_CODE": "111TTAA",	//组合代码

            }
```

## 新增页面-分类名称下拉框

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomClassifyServiceController.getPortGroupListData

方法参数：HashMap<String, Object> paraMap

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json
{}	//传的是空map
```

## 新增页面-组合列表框（排除的组合）

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexCustomClassify/controller/ICustomClassifyServiceController/getAlreadyToGroupPortCode?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomClassifyServiceController.getAlreadyToGroupPortCode

方法参数：String c_group_code

返回值：List\<String>

### 参数示例

```json
//保留参数，不需要传
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//先调用公共组合框接口加载有权限全量的组合，然后调用此接口排除返回的组合
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": [
        "111TTAA",
        "testoyls1",
        "1212tt",
        "12121111",
        "121211",
        "1211tt"
    ],
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## B区-新增自定义分类关联

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexCustomClassify/controller/ICustomClassifyRelaServiceController/insert/list?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：ICustomGroupRelaDataServiceController.insert

方法参数：List\<BasePojo> pojoList

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json
[
    {
        "c_GROUP_NAME":"",
```

# 管控配置化开发

## 字段中英文对应关系表

| 指标类型 |           |            |
| -------- | --------- | ---------- |
|          | 0         | 组合指标   |
|          | 1         | 公共指标   |
| 监控类型 |           |            |
|          | reminder  | 检查提醒类 |
|          | threshold | 监控阈值类 |
|          | contrast  | 数据核对类 |
| 提醒类型 |           |            |
|          | warning   | 预警       |
|          | fail      | 异常       |
| 核对基准 |           |            |
|          | T1        | 数据主题T1 |
|          | T2        | 数据主题T2 |
|          | T3        | 数据主题T3 |

> 检查提醒类指标：新增页面左侧区域不显示`阈值条件`和`核对配置`
>
> 监控阈值类指标：新增页面左侧区域显示`阈值条件`
>
> 数据核对类指标：新增页面左侧区域显示`核对配置`



## A区查询

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/indexDev/controller/IIndexDevServiceController/queryAllIndexDev?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IIndexDevServiceController.queryAllIndexDev

方法参数：(空)

返回值：HashMap<String,HashMap<String,String>>

### 参数示例

```json
(无)
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "0": {	//组合指标
            "contrastIndex_zxf": "核对指标配置-zxf",	//K=指标代码，V=指标名称
            "MONITOR_BONDS_BS": "债券买卖监控",
            "MONITOR_BONDS_BS_XSHG": "债券买卖监控2",
            "TEST_INDEX": "测试指标",
            "contrast_test_jc": "比对指标测试",
            "MONITOR_BONDS_BS4": "债券买卖监控4",
            "MONITOR_BONDS_BS_XSHG1": "债券买卖监控1"
        },
        "1": {	//公共指标
            "MONITOR_BONDS_AMOUNT": "证券数量监控提醒",
            "contrast_test_public_copy": "核对类指标_copy",
            "contrast_test_public": "核对类指标",
```

## B区查询条件-数据主题下拉框

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/indexDev/controller/IIndexDevORCABIServiceController/IndexDevGetORCAServices?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IIndexDevORCABIServiceController.IndexDevGetORCAServices

方法参数：String pageSize, String pageNum, String checkState

返回值：List\<IndexDevORACServicePojo>

### 参数示例

```json
//这个地方c#是循环按500查询，如果返回的记录数<500，则退出循环，否则继续按500查询，并将pageNum++，最后将多次查询list加在一起，由于数据主题不会有太多记录，所以可以只查一次，把pageSize设置为2000，看是否合适
Body类型：x-www-form-urlencodeed
参数：pageSize=500&pageNum=1&checkState=1
说明：pageSize：页大小
	 pageNum：页号
	 checkState：上线状态
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//下拉框显示：主题代码_主题名称_主题版本
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": [
        {
            "id": "21011214033362019494",
            "creatorId": "20050416193610000016",
            "createTime": "2021-01-12 14:03:37",
            "lastEditorId": "20050416193610000016",
            "lastEditTime": "2021-01-12 14:04:03",
            "checkState": "1",
            "checkerId": "20050416193610000016",
            "checkTime": "2021-01-12 14:04:08",
            "permissions": [
                "view",
                "edit",
                "remove"
            ],
            "code": "test2021011101",	//主题代码
            "version": "1_0",			//主题版本
            "name": "test2021011101",	//主题名称
            "type": "0",
            "relId": "21011214031862013071",
            "userName": "运营管控平台",
            "sourceName": "数据主题/test2021011101",
            "url": "http://192.168.2.104:18083/api/v1/public/data-services/test2021011101",
            "checked": "true",
            "orderBy": ""
        }
    ],
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## B区查询

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/indexDev/controller/IIndexDevServiceController/queryByCondition?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IIndexDevServiceController.queryByCondition

方法参数：HashMap<String,Object> paraMap

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "dataClass":"IndexDevPojo",	//数据Pojo，写死
    "C_INDEX_CODE":"contrast_test_public,contrast_test_jc",	//指标代码，多个逗号分隔
    "C_MONITOR_TYPE":"reminder|threshold|contrast",	//监控类型，多个|分隔
    "C_TOPIC_CODE":"BI_V_N_GZ_OD_CH_HL|BI_V_N_GZ_TRADE_DS",	//主题代码，多个|分隔
    "C_TOPIC_VER":"20201212|20201127",	//主题版本，多个|分隔
    "N_CHECK_STATE":"SearchAll"	//审核状态，SearchAll：所有，SearchAudit：已审核，SearchUnAudit：未审核
}
```

## 新增页面-选择数据主题时触发，数据显示在下面表格

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/indexDev/controller/IIndexDevORCABIServiceController/IndexDevGetORCAServiceInfo?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IIndexDevORCABIServiceController.IndexDevGetORCAServiceInfo

方法参数：String code, String version

返回值：List\<IndexDevORACServicePojo>

### 参数示例

```json
Body类型：x-www-form-urlencodeed
参数：code=ceshizhuti_shujuzidian_zxf&version=V1
说明：code：主题代码
	 version：主题版本
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "id": "",
        "fields": [
            {
                "id": "20081514383802494726",
                "serviceId": "20081514065802435258",
                "name": "C_AUTH_ORG_CODE",	//字段名
                "innerName": "C_AUTH_ORG_CODE",
                "type": "String",	//字段类型
                "alias": "权限组织机构"	//别名
            }
        ],
        "parameters": [	//主题参数，显示在主题基础参数列表
            {
                "id": "20081514383802494733",
                "serviceId": "20081514065802435258",
                "name": "name",	//主题参数
                "type": "String",	//类型
                "defaultValue": "正常记录数",	//条件值
                "operator": "!="	//条件
            }
        ]
    },
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```

## 下载配置化指标源代码

### 方法说明

方法名：IIndexDevServiceController.downloadIndexSourceCode

方法参数：List\<String> indexCodeList

返回值：IndexDevJar

### 参数示例

```json
//B区勾选的指标代码，未审核的也可以下载
[
    "contrastIndex_zxf",
    "MONITOR_BONDS_BS_XSHG"
]
```

```json
    "data": {

            {
                "b_FileBytes": "文件内容",

                "n_Count": 1,
                "c_FileName": "com.yss.ocp.dev.contrastIndex_zxf.zip"
            },
            {
                "b_FileBytes": "文件内容",
                "n_Index": 0,
                "n_Count": 1,
                "c_FileName": "com.yss.ocp.dev.MONITOR_BONDS_BS_XSHG.zip"
            }
        ],
        "reMap": {
            "sucIndexFilePath": [
                "com.yss.ocp.dev.contrastIndex_zxf.zip",
                "com.yss.ocp.dev.MONITOR_BONDS_BS_XSHG.zip"
            ],
            "failIndexDeployLog": [
                "下载错误的指标1的提示信息",
```

# 管控主题模板

方法名：IIndexDevTopicPlanServiceController.queryByCondition

方法参数：HashMap<String,Object> paraMap

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

```json
    "dataClass":"IndexDevTopicPlanPojo"
}
```

## 根据方案代码查询主题方案-单击A区子节点

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/indexDev/controller/IIndexDevTopicPlanServiceController/queryIndexDevTopicViewPlan?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IIndexDevTopicPlanServiceController.queryIndexDevTopicViewPlan

方法参数：String planCode

返回值：IndexDevTopicPlanViewPojo

### 参数示例

```json
ceshifangan1_z	//主题方案代码
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//显示在B区，如果是单击A区父节点，则B区表头显示A区查询返回的headList数据，如果是单击A区子节点，则B区表头固定显示，参考C#
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "indexDevTopicPlanPojo": {
            "id": "82",
            "modifier": "zxf",
            "modifyDate": "20200815 14:48:17",
            "startUseDate": "2021-01-22 13:19:04",
            "endUseDate": "2021-01-22 13:19:04",
            "auditState": 1,
            "operator": "zxf",
            "auditDate": "20200815 14:48:23",
            "topicCode": "ceshizhuti_shujuzidian_zxf",
            "topicName": "测试主题-数据字典-赵",
            "topicPlanCode": "ceshifangan1_z",
            "topicPlanName": "测试指标1_赵",
            "topicVer": "V1"
        },
        "indexDevPlanFieldList": [	//已启用的主题字段
            {
                "id": "321",
                "fieldCode": "C_AUTH_ORG_CODE",
                "fieldName": "权限组织机构",
                "fieldType": "String",
                "topicPlanCode": "ceshifangan1_z"
            }
        ],
        "indexDevPlanParameterList": [	//主题条件参数
            {
                "id": "275",
                "paramCode": "name",
                "paramCondition": "!=",
                "paramValue": "正常记录数",
                "topicPlanCode": "ceshifangan1_z"
            }
        ]
    },
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 查看主题方案（复制）-双击B区记录

基本信息-调用上面的接口

主题设置-调用管控配置化开发中2个接口，数据主题下拉框和显示表格数据



## 保存主题方案

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/indexDev/controller/IIndexDevTopicPlanServiceController/addIndexDevTopicPlan?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IIndexDevTopicPlanServiceController.addIndexDevTopicPlan

方法参数：IndexDevTopicPlanViewPojo topicPlanViewPojo

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json

    "indexDevTopicPlanPojo":{

        "topicPlanVer":null,
        "topicVer":"20201212",

        "PlanDisplayText":"jc123_jc123",	//主题方案代码_主题方案名称
        "auditState":0,
        "operator":"",
        "auditDate":null,
        "modifier":"",
        "modifyDate":null,
        "id":""
    },
    "indexDevPlanFieldList":[
        {
            "fieldCode":"TOCURRENCY",
            "fieldName":"TOCURRENCY",
            "fieldType":"String",
            "topicPlanCode":"jc123",
            "id":""
        },

            "fieldCode":"BIDRATE",

            "id":""

            "fieldCode":"OFFERRATE",

            "topicPlanCode":"jc123",
            "id":""

            "paramCode":"d_date",
```

# 指标关联设置

## 数据操作说明

| 绑定状态           | 是否能绑定 | 是否能解绑 | 是否能审核 | 是否能反审核 |
| ------------------ | ---------- | ---------- | ---------- | ------------ |
| 自动绑定（未审核） | 不能绑定   | 不能解绑   | 不能审核   | 不能反审核   |
| 自动绑定（已审核） | 不能绑定   | 能解绑     | 不能审核   | 不能反审核   |
| 人工绑定（已审核） | 不能绑定   | 能解绑     | 不能审核   | 不能反审核   |
| 人工解绑（未审核） | 能绑定     | 不能解绑   | 能审核     | 不能反审核   |
| 人工解绑（已审核） | 能绑定     | 不能解绑   | 不能审核   | 不能反审核   |
| 未绑定（未审核）   | 能绑定     | 不能解绑   | 能审核     | 不能反审核   |
| 未绑定（已审核）   | 能绑定     | 不能解绑   | 不能审核   | 不能反审核   |



## 数据排序规则

在当前分组内，按照自动绑定>人工绑定>人工解绑>未绑定的顺序排列。

### 记录排序示例

| 优先级 |          |        |
| ------ | -------- | ------ |
| 1      | 自动绑定 | 未审核 |
| 2      | 自动绑定 | 已审核 |
| 3      | 人工绑定 | 已审核 |
| 4      | 人工解绑 | 未审核 |
| 5      | 人工解绑 | 已审核 |
| 6      | 未绑定   | 未审核 |
| 7      | 未绑定   | 已审核 |



## A区-组合模式查询

和公共接口-公共组合下拉框列表一样

## 每次进入页面时请求-获取组合缓存

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexRela/controller/IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController/cacheAllPort?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController.cacheAllPort

方法参数：List\<String> portCodeList

返回值：List\<PortCachePojo>

### 参数示例

```json
//组合模式A区所有的组合代码列表
[
    "SCZ226",
    "SCV460"
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": [
        {
            "portCode": "SCZ226",
            "portName": "超未来1号私募投资基金",
            "datCode": "ASS_RQFII",
            "datCls": "CLS_PT",
            "groupList": [],
            "shortNumList": []
        },
        {
            "portCode": "SCV460",
            "portName": "象渊5期私募证券投资基金",
            "datCode": "ASS_RQFII",
            "datCls": "CLS_PT",
            "groupList": [
                "0000001"
            ],
            "shortNumList": []
        }
    ],
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## B区组合模式第一次查询-获取管控参数-排除已关账的组合

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/paramConfig/controller/IMonitorSysParamServiceController/getAutoMonitorParam?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
(无)
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "PS1|PS2|PS3|PS6|PS7",	//排除产品状态是这些状态的产品
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## B区-查询关联模式数据

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexRela/controller/IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController/queryRelaModeData?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController.queryRelaModeData

方法参数：IndexRelaModeVo vo

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json
//关联模式：关联代码下面挂指标，分页时以A区勾选的关联代码为准，所以ARRAY_RELA_CODE和dictIndexMap中勾选的关联代码需要分页，其他参数不需要分页
{
    "paraMap":{
        "dataClass":"MonitorIndexInfo",	//数据Pojo对象，写死
        "RelateMode":"RelateMode",	//关联模式
        "ARRAY_INDEX_CODE":"70049_TEST",	//B区勾选的指标代码，多个逗号分隔，如果不勾选，传所有的指标
		"ARRAY_INDEX_CODE_ALL":"dev_zqqyfs,dev_zqqyfs_test1,gkkfcs,dev_3334",	//所有的指标代码，多个逗号分隔
        "ARRAY_RELA_CODE":"CLS_PT",	//A区勾选的关联代码，多个逗号分隔，如果不勾选，有提示不让查询，提示内容参考C#
        "N_CHECK_STATE":"SearchAll"	//审核状态
    },
    "dictIndexMap":{
        "CLS_PT":"普通型"	//A区勾选的关联代码，K=关联代码，V=关联名称
    }
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "dataList": [
            {	//父节点
                "id": "",
                "modifier": "",
                "startUseDate": "2021-01-16 10:29:50",
                "endUseDate": "2021-01-16 10:29:50",
                "auditState": 0,
                "operator": "",
                "relaCode": "CLS_PT",	//关联代码
```

## B区-查询组合模式数据

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexRela/controller/IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController/queryPortModeData?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController.queryPortModeData

方法参数：IndexRelaModeVo vo

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json
//组合模式：组合下面挂指标，分页时以A区勾选的组合为准，所以ARRAY_PORT_CODE中勾选的组合需要分页，其他参数不需要分页
{
    "paraMap":{
        "dataClass":"MonitorIndexInfo",	//数据Pojo对象，写死
        "PortMode":"PortMode",	//组合模式
        "C_BIND_STATE":"ocp_handBind,ocp_autoBind,ocp_notBind,ocp_handUnbind",	//绑定状态，多个逗号分隔，如果不勾选，传所有的绑定状态
        "ARRAY_INDEX_CODE":"70049_TEST",	//B区勾选的指标代码，多个逗号分隔，如果不勾选，传所有的指标
        "ARRAY_PORT_CODE":"SCM563",	//A区勾选的组合代码，多个逗号分隔，如果不勾选，有提示不让查询，提示内容参考C#
        "N_CHECK_STATE":"SearchAll"	//审核状态
    },
    "dictIndexMap":{	//所有的指标，K=指标代码，V=指标名称
        "dev_zqqyfs":"证券权益发生",
        "dev_zqqyfs_test1":"证券权益发生提醒1",
        "gkkfcs":"管控开发测试指标",
        "dev_3334":"334",
        "dev_wbs_test11":"证券权益发生TEST11",
        "dev_wbs_test12":"证券权益发12",
        "dev_3335":"3335"
    },
    "cacheAllPortList":[	//所有缓存的组合列表
        {
            "portCode":"SCZ226",	//组合代码
            "portName":"超未来1号私募投资基金",	//组合名称
            "datCode":"ASS_RQFII",	//资产类型
            "datCls":"CLS_PT",	//资产类别
            "groupList":[	//群组代码列表
				"001",
                "002"
            ],
            "shortNumList":[	//自定义分类代码列表
				"00001",
                "00002"
            ]
        }
    ]
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "dataList": [
            {	//父节点
                "id": "",
                "modifier": "",
                "startUseDate": "2021-01-16 10:15:07",
                "endUseDate": "2021-01-16 10:15:07",
                "auditState": 0,
                "operator": "",
                "portCode": "SCM563",	//组合代码
                "portName": "阿甘2号多策略私募基金",	//组合名称
                "remark": "[SCM563]阿甘2号多策略私募基金（自动绑定 15 个，人工绑定 1 个，人工解绑 0 个，未绑定 13 个）"
            },
            {	//子节点
                "id": "",
                "modifier": "ht",
                "modifyDate": "20201225 10:59:26",
                "startUseDate": "2021-01-16 10:15:07",

                "portCode": "SCM563",

                "indexCode": "70049_TEST",	//有指标代码的就是子节点
                "indexName": "70049_TEST",
                "relaCode": "CLS_PT",

            }
        ],
        "headKeyList": [
            {
                "key": "Operate",
```

## B区-查询指标模式数据

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexRela/controller/IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController/queryIndexModeData?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController.queryIndexModeData

方法参数：IndexRelaModeVo vo

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json
//指标模式：指标下面挂组合，分页时以A区勾选的指标为准，所以ARRAY_INDEX_CODE和dictIndexMap中勾选的指标需要分页，其他参数不需要分页
{
    "paraMap":{
        "dataClass":"MonitorIndexInfo",	//数据Pojo对象，写死
        "IndexMode":"IndexMode",	//指标模式
        "C_BIND_STATE":"ocp_notBind,ocp_handUnbind,ocp_handBind,ocp_autoBind",//绑定状态，多个逗号分隔，如果不勾选，传所有的绑定状态
        "ARRAY_PORT_CODE":"SCR722",	//B区勾选的组合代码，多个逗号分隔，如果不勾选，传所有的组合代码
        "ARRAY_INDEX_CODE":"70049_TEST,80003_TEST_FAIL_PUBLIC",	//A区勾选的组合代码，多个逗号分隔
        "ARRAY_PUBLIC_INDEX_CODE":"80003_TEST_FAIL_PUBLIC",	//A区中如果勾选有公共指标，加进去，如果没有公共指标，该项参数可以不要，多个逗号分割
        "N_CHECK_STATE":"SearchAudit"	//审核状态
    },
    "dictIndexMap":{	//A区勾选的指标，K=指标代码，V=指标名称
        "70049_TEST":"70049_TEST"
    },
    "cacheAllPortList":[	//所有缓存的组合列表
        {
            "portCode":"SCZ226",
            "portName":"超未来1号私募投资基金",
            "datCode":"ASS_RQFII",
            "datCls":"CLS_PT",
            "groupList":[

            ],
            "shortNumList":[

            ]
        }
    ]
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//对于公共指标，没有子节点数据，只显示父节点
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "dataList": [
            {	//父节点
                "id": "",
                "modifier": "",
                "startUseDate": "2021-01-16 10:38:30",
                "endUseDate": "2021-01-16 10:38:30",
                "auditState": 0,
                "operator": "",
                "indexCode": "70049_TEST",	//指标代码
                "indexName": "70049_TEST",	//指标名称
                "remark": "[70049_TEST]70049_TEST（自动绑定 486 个，人工绑定 0 个，人工解绑 1 个，未绑定 10 个）"
            },
            {	//子节点
                "id": "",
                "modifier": "ht",
                "modifyDate": "20201225 10:59:26",
                "startUseDate": "2021-01-16 10:38:30",
                "endUseDate": "2021-01-16 10:38:30",
                "auditState": 1,
                "operator": "ht",
                "auditDate": "20201225 10:59:26",
                "portCode": "SCR722",	//有组合代码的就是子节点
                "portName": "曼行1号私募投资基金",
                "indexCode": "70049_TEST",
                "indexName": "70049_TEST",
                "relaCode": "CLS_PT",
                "relaName": "普通型",
                "bindState": "ocp_autoBind",
                "relaType": "ocp_datRela"
            }
        ],
        "headKeyList": [
            {
                "key": "Operate",
                "text": "操作",
                "align": "L",
                "format": "",
                "serviceId": "",
                "showName": "",
                "isShow": "",
                "width": "",
                "sortable": "",
                "order": "",
                "isExport": "",
                "isFrozen": "",
                "typeCode": "",
                "defaultDictTypeValue": "",
                "dictType": ""
            },
            {
                "key": "PortCode",
                "text": "组合代码",
                "align": "L",
                "format": "",
                "serviceId": "",
                "showName": "",
                "isShow": "",
                "width": "",
                "sortable": "",
                "order": "",
                "isExport": "",
                "isFrozen": "",
                "typeCode": "",
                "defaultDictTypeValue": "",
                "dictType": ""
            },
            {
                "key": "PortName",
                "text": "组合名称",
                "align": "L",

                "serviceId": "",
                "showName": "",
                "isShow": "",
                "width": "",
                "sortable": "",
                "order": "",
                "isExport": "",
                "isFrozen": "",
                "typeCode": "",
                "defaultDictTypeValue": "",
                "dictType": ""
            },
            {
                "key": "RelaType",
                "text": "关联模式",
                "align": "L",
                "format": "",
                "serviceId": "IVocDataService",
                "showName": "",
                "isShow": "",
                "width": "",
                "sortable": "",
```

## 绑定

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexRela/controller/IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController/bind?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

方法名：IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController.bind

方法参数：List\<MonitorIndexInfo> dataList

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json

[
    {
        "relaCode":null,
        "relaName":"",
        "remark":null,
        "bindState":"ocp_notBind",
        "relaType":"ocp_unRela",

        "portName":"ETF测试用",

        "planCode":null,
        "planName":null,

        "endUseDate":"2021-01-16 10:48:58",
```

## 保存关联模式数据

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexRela/controller/IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController/saveRelaInfo?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

方法参数：HashMap<String, Object> paraMap

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "SearchType":"ocp_datRela",	//选择的资产类别代码
    "ARRAY_INDEX_CODE":"80002_TEST_WARN_PUB&&80002_TEST_WARN_PUB",	//要保存的指标，多个逗号分隔，&&分隔指标代码和指标名称
    "ARRAY_RELA_CODE":"CLS_LJ&&联接型,CLS_PT&&普通型"	//要保存的关联代码，多个逗号分隔，&&分隔关联代码和关联名称
}
```

```json

    "code": "success",
```

## B区-组合模式局部刷新

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexRela/controller/IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController/queryPortModeDataByRefresh?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController.queryPortModeDataByRefresh

方法参数：IndexRelaModeVo vo

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json
//绑定，解绑，审核，都需要局部刷新，哪个模式下就调对应的接口
//组合模式的局部刷新，K=组合代码，V=指标代码，多个逗号分隔，如果有多个组合，就再加一个键值对
{
    "paraMap":{
        "SCZ395":"dev_3334,GZ45_HLD,STOCK_GZJGBDFDJC"
    },
    "dictIndexMap":{	//所有的指标，K=指标代码，V=指标名称
        "dev_zqqyfs":"证券权益发生",
        "dev_zqqyfs_test1":"证券权益发生提醒1",
        "gkkfcs":"管控开发测试指标",
        "dev_3334":"334",
        "dev_wbs_test11":"证券权益发生TEST11",
        "dev_wbs_test12":"证券权益发12",
        "dev_3335":"3335"
    },
    "cacheAllPortList":[	//所有缓存的组合列表
        {
            "portCode":"SCZ226",
            "portName":"超未来1号私募投资基金",
            "datCode":"ASS_RQFII",
            "datCls":"CLS_PT",

            ],
            "shortNumList":[

            ]
        }
    ]
}
```

## B区-指标模式局部刷新

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexRela/controller/IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController/queryIndexModeDataByRefresh?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController.queryIndexModeDataByRefresh

方法参数：IndexRelaModeVo vo

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json
//绑定，解绑，审核，都需要局部刷新，哪个模式下就调对应的接口
//指标模式的局部刷新，K=指标代码，V=组合代码，多个逗号分隔，如果有多个指标，就再加一个键值对
{
    "paraMap":{
        "70049_TEST":"159948,513600,510290"
    },
    "dictIndexMap":{	//勾选的指标，K=指标代码，V=指标名称
        "70049_TEST":"70049_TEST"
    },
    "cacheAllPortList":[	//所有缓存的组合列表
        {
            "portCode":"SCZ226",
            "portName":"超未来1号私募投资基金",
            "datCode":"ASS_RQFII",
            "datCls":"CLS_PT",
            "groupList":[

            ],
            "shortNumList":[

            ]
        }
    ]
}
```

## B区-关联模式局部刷新

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexRela/controller/IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController/queryByIds/map?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
//审核、反审核、删除，都需要局部刷新
//关联模式的局部刷新根据id来刷新
{
    "dataClass":"MonitorIndexInfo",
    "ids":"8037,8036"	//行数据中的id，多个逗号分割
}
```

# 指标信息管理

## A区查询

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/monitorIndex/controller/IMonitorIndexConfigServiceController/queryByCondition?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IMonitorIndexConfigServiceController.queryByCondition

方法参数：HashMap<String, Object> paraMap

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "dataClass":"MonitorIndex",	//数据pojo，写死
    "searchType":"INDEX_TYPE",	//写死
    "searchMenu":"monitorIndexConfig"	//写死
}
```

## A区-拖拽更改指标分类

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/monitorIndex/controller/IMonitorIndexConfigServiceController/updateDragData?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "index":{
        "indexCode":"test1234",	//指标代码或分类代码
        "indexName":"test1234",	//指标名称或分类名称
        "indexType":null,
        "indexParams":null,
        "indexDesc":null,
        "isPublic":null,
        "mergeType":null,
        "indexKey":null,
        "fileName":null,
        "state":null,
        "confirm":null,
        "typeCode":"test",	//拖拽后的上级分类代码，根节点为:[root]
        "typeName":null,
        "typeP":null,
        "indexAlias":null,
        "datCode":null,
        "datCls":null,
        "paramValue":null,
        "deployBy":null,
        "deployTime":null,
        "executeFunCodes":null,
        "version":null,
        "paramConfigList":null,
        "installState":null,
        "thirdDataType":null,
        "cfgCode":null,
        "productLine":null,
        "devMode":null,
        "riskLevel":null,
        "indexLevel":null,
        "indexParent":null,
        "portLevel":null,
        "remark":null,
        "entranceClass":null,
        "entranceContext":null,
        "indexOrder":0,
        "existParams":0,
        "executeBizCodesDb":null,
        "detailDescList":null,
        "sortColumns":null,
        "paramExtendList":null,
        "auditState":1,
        "operator":"",
        "auditDate":null,
        "modifier":"",
        "modifyDate":null,
        "id":"487"
    },
    "flag":"True"	//True表示拖拽的是分类，False表示拖拽的是指标
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000006\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":\"monitorIndexConfig\",\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{},\"cidenList\":[]}}",
```

## B区上半部分查询

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/monitorIndex/controller/IMonitorIndexConfigServiceController/queryByCondition/page?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IMonitorIndexConfigServiceController.queryByCondition

方法参数：RestfulQueryConditionVo restfulQueryConditionVo

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "paraMap":{
        "TypeQuery":"TypeQuery",	//写死
        "IndexCode":"ACT_ETFTZGLQSXXWZXJC",	//A区勾选的指标代码，多个逗号分隔
        "searchMenu":"monitorIndexConfig",	//写死
        "dataClass":"MonitorIndex"	//数据pojo，写死
    },
    "page":{	//分页信息
        "currPage":1,
        "pageCount":0,
        "totalNum":1,
        "pageSize":100,
        "usePage":true
    }
}
```

## B区上半部分指标详情-指标类型下拉框（上面接口返回true才执行此请求）

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
[
    "PORT_LEVEL"
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//如果上一个请求返回false，则不执行此请求，指标类型是文本框，值根据isPublic来显示，0显示组合指标，1显示公共指标，且不可编辑
//如果上一个请求返回true，则执行此请求，指标类型是下拉框，值填此请求返回的内容，且可以编辑

    "code": "success",
    "data": [
```

请求方式：POST

方法参数：RestfulQueryConditionVo restfulQueryConditionVo

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json

    "paraMap":{
        "indexCode":"ACT_ETFTZGLQSXXWZXJC",	//指标代码
```

## 指标变更记录-B区下半部分查询（单击B区上半部分行数据）

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexDesc/controller/IOcpIndexModifyRecordServiceController/queryByCondition?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IOcpIndexModifyRecordServiceController/queryByCondition

方法参数：HashMap<String, Object> paraMap

返回值：RestfulQueryResult

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "indexCode":"ACT_ETFTZGLQSXXWZXJC",	//指标代码
    "dataClass":"OcpIndexModifyRecord",	//数据pojo，写死
    "N_CHECK_STATE":"SearchAll"	//如果是单击B区上半部分的记录，固定传SearchAll，如果是点下方的查询按钮后的审核和未审核，则传对应的，见上面
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "dataList": [
            {
                "id": "143",
                "modifier": "ht",	//制作人
```

## 指标功能描述-B区下半部分修改行数据

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexDesc/controller/IOcpIndexDescServiceController/updateById/list?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IOcpIndexDescServiceController.updateById

方法参数：List\<OcpIndexDesc> pojoList

返回值：String

### 参数示例

```json
//数组只有一个元素，一行记录
[
    {
        "indexCode":"ACT_ETFTZGLQSXXWZXJC",
        "indexName":"ETF台账关联券商信息完成性检查",
        "indexDesc":"发生大发大是范德萨发的沙发as ",
        "indexRule":"asd",
        "applyCode":"zh",
        "busiService":"fw",
        "accessWay":"addddf",
        "desc":"讲话稿",
        "indexStoryBy":"ht",
        "indexStoryTime":"2021-01-01 00:00:00",
        "auditState":0,
        "operator":"",
        "auditDate":null,
        "modifier":"ht",
        "modifyDate":null,
        "id":"442"
    }
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000006\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":\"ocpIndexDesc\",\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{},\"cidenList\":[]}}",
```

## 卸载指标

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexDeploy/controller/IMonitorIndexDeployServiceController/unInstall?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
//B区一行记录当参数传入,放入list，第二个参数标识是否同时删除数据

    "monitorIndexList":[
        {
            "indexCode":"MONITOR_BONDS_BS",

            "confirm":null,
            "typeCode":null,
            "typeName":null,
            "typeP":null,
            "indexAlias":"债券买卖监控",

            "datCls":"CLS_PT",
            "paramValue":null,
            "deployBy":"ht",
            "deployTime":"20201210 17:15:05",
            "executeFunCodes":"stockStats",
            "version":"1.1",
            "paramConfigList":null,
            "installState":"0",
            "thirdDataType":"0",
            "cfgCode":null,
            "productLine":null,
            "devMode":"fomp",
            "riskLevel":"low",
            "indexLevel":null,
```

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
[
    "STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX"	//指标代码，list，有多个
]
```

## 关联设置-选择关联类型后

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexRela/controller/IOcpRelaModeAreaAServiceController/getRelaModeAreaA?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
群组模式：{"SearchType":"ocp_groupRela"}
资产类型：{"SearchType":"ocp_assRela"}
资产类别：{"SearchType":"ocp_datRela"}
自定义分类：{"SearchType":"ocp_shortNumRela"}
指定组合：用公共数据中的公共组合下拉框的那个请求，这里就不重复写了
```

## 保存关联设置（包含批量设置和公共指标的自动保存）

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexDeploy/controller/IMonitorIndexDeployServiceController/setRelaMode?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
//公共指标，自动触发请求，进入关联设置界面自动触发
[
    {
        "indexCode":"IMP_ZQJBXXQSJC",
        "indexName":"证券基本信息缺失检查",
        "relaCode":null,	//公共指标以下字段不用传
        "relaName":null,
        "relaType":null,
        "updateBy":null,
        "updateTime":null,
        "checkState":0,
        "checkBy":null,
        "checkTime":null,
        "id":""
    }
]
//组合指标，手动触发请求
[
    {
        "indexCode":"STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX",
        "indexName":"浮息债券利率调整提醒",
        "relaCode":"ASS_FOF",	//组合指标，选择的关联代码
        "relaName":"FOF基金",
        "relaType":"ocp_assRela",
        "updateBy":null,
        "updateTime":null,
        "checkState":0,
        "checkBy":null,
        "checkTime":null,
        "id":""
    },
    {
        "indexCode":"STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX",
        "indexName":"浮息债券利率调整提醒",
        "relaCode":"ASS_QDII",
        "relaName":"QDII证券基金",
        "relaType":"ocp_assRela",
        "updateBy":null,
        "updateTime":null,
        "checkState":0,
        "checkBy":null,
        "checkTime":null,
        "id":""
    }
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000001\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":\"monitorIndexConfig\",\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{\"aa\":\"1\",\"bb\":\"2\"},\"cidenList\":[\"8790\",\"8791\"]}}",
```

## 参数设置-点击调整或查看（加载参数Config）

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX	//指标代码
```

```json

    "code": "success",
    "data": [

            "id": "",
```

### 控件说明

| 控件类型            | 控件说明                       |
| ------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| text                | 纯文本                         |
| YssSelCombox        | 下拉框控件                     |
| YssTextBox          | 文本框控件                     |
| ImprovedTextBox     | 带前后缀的文本控件             |
| SubsectionTextBox   | 范围型控件                     |
| YssDateTimeInterval | 日期控件                       |
| QuickLink           | 扩展参数链接，点击打开扩展参数 |

### 字段属性说明

|                              |                                                              |                                                              |
| ---------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------ |
| name                         | 名称列                                                       |                                                              |
| condition                    | 条件列                                                       |                                                              |
| value                        | 值列                                                         |                                                              |
| desc                         | 描述列                                                       |                                                              |
|                              |                                                              |                                                              |
| code                         | 对应上面的4列                                                |                                                              |
| type                         | 控件类型                                                     |                                                              |
| config                       | 控件配置                                                     |                                                              |
| val                          | 控件值                                                       |                                                              |
|                              |                                                              |                                                              |
| value                        |                                                              |                                                              |
| serviceId                    | type=”YssSelCombox”时的专用属性，下拉框的数据源，IVocDataService，IMonitorIndexDropDownService，IOcpIndexDropDownService |                                                              |
| methodName                   | type=”YssSelCombox”时的专用属性，下拉框数据源的请求方法      |                                                              |
| methodParams                 | type=”YssSelCombox”时的专用属性，下拉框数据源的请求方法参数  |                                                              |
| kTableTree                   | type=”YssSelCombox”时的专用属性，下拉框是否树形展示，默认false |                                                              |
| multiSelect                  | type=”YssSelCombox”时的专用属性，下拉框是否多选，默认false   |                                                              |
| displayStyel                 | type=”YssSelCombox”时的专用属性，下拉框展示方式，DropDown下拉、Modal对话框，默认DropDown |                                                              |
| fixStyle                     | type=”ImprovedTextBox”或”SubsectionTextBox”时的专用属性，fixStyle=“Sufix”表示后缀控件，Prefix表示前缀控件 |                                                              |
| fixValue                     | type=”ImprovedTextBox”或”SubsectionTextBox”时的专用属性，前/后缀的内容 |                                                              |
| length                       | type=”ImprovedTextBox”或“YssTextBox”或”SubsectionTextBox”的专用属性，文本长度 |                                                              |
| numeric                      | type=”ImprovedTextBox”或“YssTextBox”或”SubsectionTextBox”的专用属性，控件内容为数值时，数值的精度 |                                                              |
| isMust                       | 控件是否必输，默认true                                       |                                                              |
| defaultVal                   | type=”ImprovedTextBox”或“YssTextBox”或”SubsectionTextBox”或"YssDateTimeInterval"的属性，默认值，日期控件格式为YYYY-MM-DD |                                                              |
| isRangeType                  | 是否开启范围型控件，True开启；false不开启（范围型控件开启需要methodParams="YJJK_NR"） |                                                              |
|                              |                                                              |                                                              |
| IVocDataService              | /osgi-fast/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/platform/support/dataservice/controller/IVocDataServiceController/getDataListByTypes?serviceId=osgi-fast | ["YJJK_ZF"]                                                  |
| IMonitorIndexDropDownService | /yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/monitorIndex/controller/IMonitorIndexDropDownServiceController/getDropDownInfos?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor | getInterfaceCodes                                            |
| IOcpIndexDropDownService     | /yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexParam/controller/IOcpIndexDropDownServiceController/getDropDownInfos?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor | {"methodName":"getSecVarCodes","paraMap":{"C_SEC_VAR_CODE":"FZ"}} |



## 参数设置-点击调整或查看（加载参数Val）

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexDeploy/controller/IMonitorIndexDeployServiceController/loadParamVal?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
Body类型：x-www-form-urlencodeed
参数：indexCode=STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX&relaCode=-&relaType=-
说明：indexCode：指标代码
	 relaCode：关联代码
	 relaType：关联类型
```

## 参数设置-删除参数

### 方法说明

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
Body类型：x-www-form-urlencodeed
参数：indexCode=STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX&relaCode=ocp_assRela&relaType=ASS_FOF
说明：indexCode：指标代码
	 relaCode：关联代码
	 relaType：关联类型
```

## 参数设置-新增扩展参数

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexDeploy/controller/IMonitorIndexDeployServiceController/saveParamData?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "indexCode":"STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX",
    "paramID":"secCodeList",
    "condition":{
        "C_SEC_VAR_CODE":"LL",
        "C_DA_CODE":"LL",
        "C_SEC_CODE":"1233.00",
        "C_SEC_NAME":"43123",
        "C_UPDATE_BY":"ht",
        "C_RELA_TYPE":"ocp_assRela",
        "C_RELA_CODE":"ASS_FOF",
        "C_RELA_TYPE_NEW":"ocp_assRela",
        "C_RELA_CODE_NEW":"ASS_FOF"
    }
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000001\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":\"monitorIndexConfig\",\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{\"aa\":\"1\",\"bb\":\"2\"},\"cidenList\":[\"23\"]}}",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 参数设置-删除扩展参数

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexDeploy/controller/IMonitorIndexDeployServiceController/deleteParamData?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "indexCode":"STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX",
    "paramID":"secCodeList",
    "ids":"22",
    "condition":{
        "C_RELA_TYPE":"ocp_assRela",
        "C_RELA_CODE":"ASS_FOF",
        "C_RELA_TYPE_NEW":"ocp_assRela",
        "C_RELA_CODE_NEW":"ASS_FOF"
    }
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000002\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":\"monitorIndexConfig\",\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{},\"cidenList\":[]}}",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 参数设置-修改扩展参数

### 方法说明

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "indexCode":"STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX",
    "paramID":"secCodeList",
    "condition":{
        "C_SEC_VAR_CODE":"LL",
        "C_DA_CODE":"LL",
        "C_SEC_CODE":"1233.00",
        "C_SEC_NAME":"21312",

        "C_IDEN":"23",

        "C_RELA_CODE":"ASS_FOF",
        "C_RELA_TYPE_NEW":"ocp_assRela",

    }
}
```

## 载入配置化指标-点击管控配置化开发页面的部署自动生成指标

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/indexDev/controller/IIndexDevServiceController/autoProduceIndex?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

方法名：IIndexDevServiceController.autoProduceIndex

方法参数：List\<String> indexCodeList

返回值：Map<String, List\<String>>

### 参数示例

```json
//B区勾选的指标，未审核的也可以勾选，会有提示日志，未审核不让部署
[
    "contrast_test_jc",
    "contrast_test_public",
    "contrastIndex_zxf",
    "contrast_test_public_copy"
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "sucIndexFilePath": [
            "com.yss.ocp.dev.contrast_test_jc_1.300.7-20210210.jar",	//文件名传到下一个请求
            "com.yss.ocp.dev.contrast_test_public_1.300.7-20210210.jar"
        ],
        "failIndexDeployLog": [
            "配置化指标[contrastIndex_zxf]打包失败：指标未审核，无法进行打包！",
            "配置化指标[contrast_test_public_copy]打包失败：指标未审核，无法进行打包！"
        ]
    },
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```

## 灰度上线-刷新缓存

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexDeploy/controller/IMonitorIndexDeployServiceController/refreshCanaryCache?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
//点灰度上线，灰度上线的指标
[
    "STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX"
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//返回值不用关心
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



# 指标灰度上线

```json
(无)
```

## 试运行-执行

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/controller/IMonitoringExecuteServiceController/check?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "portCodes":[	//B区勾选的组合
        "qqqqq",
        "asdasdc"
    ],
    "indexCodes":[	//待上线指标中勾选的指标
        "MONITOR_BONDS_BS"
    ],
    "strDate":"2021-02-04",	//日期
    "executeId":"e59b99d8-2002-4b87-9d07-706d34ff5648",	//需要前端随机生成UUID，注意用postman测试时，每次调用此请求时要保证此executeId唯一
    "strExecuteMode":"CheckRun",	//写死
    "isCanary":"true"	//true：待上线指标试运行，false：已上线指标试运行
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//返回值固定为空，这里实际上是发送一个执行请求，后台会多线程调度执行
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 试运行-拿进度

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/controller/IMonitoringExecuteServiceController/getProgress?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
e59b99d8-2002-4b87-9d07-706d34ff5648	//上一步的executeId
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//此请求会每隔500ms调一次，直到completNum=total相等，如果不相等，一直拿这两个值，刷新底部进度条，如果相等，则取最后一次请求的结果展示在B区
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "total": 2,	//总数
        "indexCheckResults": [	//检查结果
            {
                "id": "",
                "excuteId": "e59b99d8-2002-4b87-9d07-706d34ff5648",
                "bizDate": "2021-02-04 00:00:00",
                "indexCode": "MONITOR_BONDS_BS",
                "indexName": "债券买卖监控",
                "resultTitle": "债券买卖监控 【失败】 ",	//结果标题
                "resultState": "0",	//总结果状态，0：失败，1：成功
                "sysCheckResultList": {	//系统环境检测明细结果
                    "0": [
                        "未找到FOMP执行节点，请检查是否启动！"
                    ],
                    "1":[
                        
                    ]
                },
                "sysCheckState": "0",	//系统环境检测结果，0：失败，1：成功
                "runCheckResultList":{
                    "0":[
                        
                    ],
                	"1":[
                        
                    ]
                },
                "runCheckState": "0",	//试运行检测结果，0：失败，1：成功
                "updateBy": "ht",
                "updateTime": "2021-02-04 15:07:26",
                "c_isCanary": "1"
            }
        ],
        "completNum": 2	//完成数
    },
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 待上线指标-正式上线

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/controller/IMonitoringExecuteServiceController/releaseIndex?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
//只能勾选试运行成功的指标，待试运行和试运行失败的指标不允许上线，不处理就行，执行完上线后，刷新A区
[
    "70049_TEST"
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "70049_TEST": "1"	//1表示成功，如果失败就是详细的错误信息，直接输出
    },
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



# 指标参数设置

## A区-组合模式查询

同公共组合框



## A区-指标模式查询

同指标关联设置的指标模式A区，如果指标分类中没有指标，则不显示该分类



## B区-生效参数下拉框

查看公共接口



## 每次进入页面时请求-获取组合缓存

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexRela/controller/IMonitorIndexRelaServiceController/cacheAllPort?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
//A区所有的组合代码
[
    "777888",
    "SM9375"
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//将返回的值缓存，B区查询时当参数传入
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": [
        {
            "portCode": "777888",
            "portName": "ROY融资融券",
            "datCode": "ASS_ZCGLJH",
            "datCls": "CLS_PT",
            "groupList": [],
            "shortNumList": []
        },
        {
            "portCode": "SM9375",
            "portName": "合盈趋势稳增2号私募基金",
            "datCode": "ASS_ZCGLJH",
            "datCls": "CLS_PT",
            "groupList": [],
            "shortNumList": []
        }
    ],
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## B区组合模式第一次查询-获取管控参数-排除已关账的组合

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/paramConfig/controller/IMonitorSysParamServiceController/getAutoMonitorParam?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
(无)
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "PS1|PS2|PS3|PS6|PS7",	//排除产品状态是这些状态的产品
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## B区-查询

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexParam/controller/IOcpIndexParamServiceController/queryIndexParamList?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
//组合模式：
//1、无参数只能查看
//2、所有的指标参数和分类参数（包含审核和未审核）都可以调整
//3、所有的指标参数和分类参数（包含审核和未审核）都不允许审核和反审核操作，提示信息参考C#输出
//4、所有的可以调整的参数，调整完后都变成私有参数
//5、只有私有参数才能审核和反审核
//6、已审核的私有参数，不能调整
//指标模式：
//1、所有的指标参数、分类参数、私有参数都可以审核和反审核
//2、已审核的参数，不能调整
//3、除子节点的第一行记录，指标参数调整完后，会变成对应的参数，如：关联信息如果是群组，则调整完后变成分类参数，如果是指定组合，则调整完后变成私有参数
//4、无参数的，子节点只显示一行
{
    "paraMap":{	//组合模式
        "dataClass":"OcpIndexParam",	//写死
        "SearchMode":"PortMode",	//组合模式，写死
        "ARRAY_INDEX_CODE":"80001_TEST_SUCCESS,80002_TEST_WARN",	//B区选择的指标，多个逗号分割，如果不勾选，传所有的指标
        "ARRAY_PORT_CODE":"111TTAA",	//A区选择的组合，如果不勾选，有提示不让查询，提示内容参考C#
        "C_PARAM_TYPE":"ocp_indexParam,ocp_groupParam,ocp_portParam,ocp_noParam",	//B区生效参数，如果不勾选，传所有的生效参数
        "N_CHECK_STATE":"SearchAll"	//审核状态
    },
    "paraMap":{	//指标模式
        "dataClass":"OcpIndexParam",	//写死
        "SearchMode":"IndexMode",	//指标模式，写死
        "ARRAY_INDEX_CODE":"80002_TEST_WARN,80003_TEST_FAIL_PUBLIC",	//A区选择的指标，多个逗号分割，如果不勾选，有提示不让查询，提示内容参考C#
        "ARRAY_PUBLIC_INDEX_CODE":"80003_TEST_FAIL_PUBLIC",	//A区中如果勾选有公共指标，加进去，如果没有公共指标，该项参数可以不要，多个逗号分割
        "C_PARAM_TYPE":"ocp_indexParam,ocp_groupParam,ocp_portParam,ocp_noParam",	//B区生效参数，如果不勾选，传所有的生效参数
        "N_CHECK_STATE":"SearchAll"	//审核状态
    },
    "dictIndexMap":{	//组合模式，传所有指标，K=指标代码，V=指标名称，指标模式，传勾选的指标
        "STOCK_GZQHJEHD":"期货备付/保证金核对",
        "ACT_FHBJJDRFHJK":"场外非货币基金当日分红监控"
    },
    "cacheAllPortList":[	//组合缓存
        {
            "portCode":"777888",
            "portName":"ROY融资融券",
            "datCode":"ASS_ZCGLJH",
            "datCls":"CLS_PT",
            "groupList":[

            ],
            "shortNumList":[

            ]
        }
    ]
}
```

### 返回值示例

## B区-查看/调整-查询指标详情

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexParam/controller/IOcpIndexParamServiceController/queryIndexBaseInfo?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
STOCK_JZRJZBDJC	//指标代码
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "id": "4485",
        "modifier": "ht",
        "modifyDate": "20210224 10:16:10",
        "startUseDate": "2021-02-26 11:55:05",
        "endUseDate": "2021-02-26 11:55:05",
        "auditState": 1,
        "operator": "ht",
        "auditDate": "20210224 11:46:44",
        "indexCode": "80003_TEST_FAIL",
        "indexName": "80003_TEST_FAIL",
        "entranceClass": "com.yss.ams.monitor.nosql_test.execute.testIndex",
        "entranceContext": "com.yss.uco.monitor.support.index.MonitoringContext",
        "indexOrder": 1,
        "indexType": "统计分析",
```

## B区-查询参数详细信息-Config

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/monitorIndex/controller/IMonitorIndexConfigServiceController/getParamConfigByIndex?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
80002_TEST_WARN	//指标代码
```

## B区-查询参数详细信息-Val

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexParam/controller/IOcpIndexParamServiceController/queryIndexParamVal?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
Body类型：x-www-form-urlencodeed
参数：indexCode=80002_TEST_WARN&relaCode=-&relaType=-
说明：indexCode：指标代码
	 relaCode：关联代码，行数据中的paramRelaCode
	 relaType：关联类型，行数据中的paramRelaType
```

### 返回值示例


## B区-更新保存参数

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexParam/controller/IOcpIndexParamServiceController/updateIndexParamVal?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
[
    {
        "portCode":null,
        "indexCode":"80001_TEST_SUCCESS",
        "planCode":null,
        "paramID":"P1",
        "paramType":null,
        "nameCode":"name",
        "nameVal":"检查包含全价报价债券",
        "conditionCode":"condition",
        "conditionVal":"等于",
        "valueCode":"value",
        "valueVal":"0",
        "descCode":"desc",
        "descVal":"用于控制在取估值表债券持仓时，是否要排除债券的报价方式为全价的债品",
        "relaType":"-",	//当前参数，paramRelaType
        "relaCode":"-",	//当前参数，paramRelaType
        "newRelaType":"ocp_portRela",	//新的参数，组合模式：relaType，指标模式：relaType
        "newRelaCode":"111TTAA",	//新的参数，组合模式：parentCode，指标模式：relaCode
        "id":""
    },
    {
        "portCode":null,
        "indexCode":"80001_TEST_SUCCESS",
        "planCode":null,
        "paramID":"P2",
        "paramType":null,
        "nameCode":"name",
        "nameVal":"检查包含全价报价债券",
        "conditionCode":"condition",
        "conditionVal":"等于",
        "valueCode":"value",
        "valueVal":"0",
        "descCode":"desc",
        "descVal":"用于控制在取估值表债券持仓时，是否要排除债券的报价方式为全价的债品",
        "relaType":"-",
        "relaCode":"-",
        "newRelaType":"ocp_portRela",
        "newRelaCode":"111TTAA",
        "id":""
    }
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000006\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":\"ocpIndexParam\",\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{},\"cidenList\":[]}}",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## B区-局部刷新

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexParam/controller/IOcpIndexParamServiceController/queryIndexParamListByRefresh?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
//审核、反审核、调整，都需要局部刷新
{
    "paraMap":{
        "SearchMode":"IndexMode",	//IndexMode：指标模式，PortMode：组合模式
        "STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX":"ASS_FOF"	//指标模式以指标代码为Key，关联代码或组合代码为Value，多个逗号分割，如果都选了子节点第一行，则V传""空串
        								//组合模式以组合代码为Key，指标代码为Value，多个逗号分割
    },
    "dictIndexMap":{	//组合模式，传所有指标，K=指标代码，V=指标名称，指标模式，传勾选的指标
        "STOCK_GZQHJEHD":"期货备付/保证金核对",
        "ACT_FHBJJDRFHJK":"场外非货币基金当日分红监控"
    },
    "cacheAllPortList":[	//组合缓存
        {
            "portCode":"777888",
            "portName":"ROY融资融券",
            "datCode":"ASS_ZCGLJH",
            "datCls":"CLS_PT",
            "groupList":[

            ],
            "shortNumList":[

            ]
        }
    ]
}
```

## 参数设置-查询扩展参数

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexParam/controller/IOcpParamExtendServiceController/queryExtendParamData?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "indexCode":"STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX",
    "paramID":"secCodeList",
    "condition":{
        "C_SEC_VAR_CODE":"CT",	//查询参数
        "C_DA_CODE":"CJ",
        "C_SEC_CODE":"123.00",
        "C_SEC_NAME":"123",
        "C_RELA_TYPE":"ocp_portRela",	//当前参数
        "C_RELA_CODE":"111TTAA"
    },
    "textBoxControl":[	//文本框需要模糊查询
        "C_SEC_NAME"
    ]
}
```

```json
    "data":{
```

## 参数设置-新增扩展参数

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/indexParam/controller/IOcpParamExtendServiceController/saveParamData?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "indexCode":"STOCK_FXZQLLTZTX",
    "paramID":"secCodeList",
    "data":{
        "C_SEC_VAR_CODE":"CT",
        "C_DA_CODE":"CT",
        "C_SEC_CODE":"123.00",
        "C_SEC_NAME":"456",
        "C_UPDATE_BY":"ht",	//当前登录用户名
        "C_RELA_TYPE":"-",	//旧参数
        "C_RELA_CODE":"-",
        "C_RELA_TYPE_NEW":"ocp_portRela",	//新参数
        "C_RELA_CODE_NEW":"111TTAA"
    }
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000001\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":\"\",\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{\"aa\":\"1\",\"bb\":\"2\"},\"cidenList\":[\"28\"]}}",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```

```json
        "C_RELA_CODE":"111TTAA",
```

```json
        "code":"ZHWHQQK",
        "name":"持仓证券无行情检查",
```

请求方式：POST

```json
(无)
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": [
        {
            "id": "",
            "c_PLAN_CODE": "3333",	//方案代码
            "c_PLAN_NAME": "3333_全选",	//方案名称
            "c_MONITOR_STATE": "Success|Fail|Warning|Pending",	//监控状态，多个|分隔
            "c_HANDLER_STATE": "0|1",	//处理状态，多个|分隔
            "c_SEARCH_MODE": "index",	//index：指标模式，port：组合模式
            "c_INDEX_CODE_LIST": [	//如果是指标模式，存的时候A区的指标代码；如果是组合模式，存的是B区的指标代码
                "70049_TEST",
                "71694_TEST",
                "NOSQL_TEST",
                "STOCK_GZQHJEHD",
                "STOCK_GZYPBCCHD",
                "STOCK_JYTCBHD",
                "STOCK_JZRJZBDJC",

            ]

            "id": "",
            "c_PLAN_CODE": "123",
            "c_PLAN_NAME": "123_123",
            "c_MONITOR_STATE": "Fail|Warning|3|0",
            "c_HANDLER_STATE": "0",
            "c_SEARCH_MODE": "port",
            "c_INDEX_CODE_LIST": [
                "70049_TEST",
                "GROOVY_DEMO_1",
```

## 查询方案增、删、改

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/summary/controller/IMonitorSummaryServiceController/updateMonitorLogQueryPlan?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "queryPlan":{
        "c_PLAN_CODE":"456",
        "c_PLAN_NAME":"456",
        "c_MONITOR_STATE":"Fail|Warning",
        "c_HANDLER_STATE":"0|1",
        "c_SEARCH_MODE":"port",
        "c_INDEX_CODE_LIST":[
            "70049_TEST",
            "80002_TEST_WARN",
            "80003_TEST_FAIL",
            "80003_TEST_FAIL_PUBLIC",
            "80001_TEST_SUCCESS"
        ],
        "id":""
    },
    "operType":"ADD"	//增加操作，如果输入的方案代码下拉框中不存在，则新增
}

{
    "queryPlan":{
        "c_PLAN_CODE":"456",
        "c_PLAN_NAME":"4567",
        "c_MONITOR_STATE":"Fail|Warning",
        "c_HANDLER_STATE":"0|1",
        "c_SEARCH_MODE":"port",
        "c_INDEX_CODE_LIST":[
            "70049_TEST",
            "80001_TEST_SUCCESS",
            "80002_TEST_WARN",
            "80003_TEST_FAIL",
            "80003_TEST_FAIL_PUBLIC"
        ],
        "id":""
    },
    "operType":"UPD"	//更新操作，如果输入的方案代码下拉框中存在，则覆盖
}

{
    "queryPlan":{
        "c_PLAN_CODE":"456",
        "c_PLAN_NAME":null,
        "c_MONITOR_STATE":null,
        "c_HANDLER_STATE":null,
        "c_SEARCH_MODE":null,
        "c_INDEX_CODE_LIST":null,
        "id":""
    },
    "operType":"DEL"	//删除操作，如果是点的删除按钮，则删除
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "JSON_INFO:{\"ret_INFO\":{\"infoCode\":\"INF-000005\",\"infoName\":null,\"infoType\":\"INFO\",\"cause\":null,\"detailMsg\":null,\"memo\":\"Success\",\"recordOperCount\":null,\"operRes\":\"Success\",\"operType\":null,\"infoGroup\":\"SYS\",\"funCode\":null,\"funName\":null,\"rootFunCode\":null,\"rootFunName\":null,\"logNo\":null,\"terminalType\":\"SV\",\"detailInfo\":null,\"infoContent\":null,\"specStrHs\":{},\"cidenList\":[]}}",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 每次进入页面时请求-获取组合缓存

同指标关联设置，一模一样



## B区-查询

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/summary/controller/IMonitorSummaryServiceController/queryByConditionNew?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "paraMap":{
        "dataClass":"MonitorSummary",	//写死
        "MONITOR_START_DATE":"2021-02-10",	//开始日期，如果只显示开始日期，则结束日期等于开始日期
        "MONITOR_END_DATE":"2021-02-10",	//结束日期
        "MONITOR_STATE":"Fail,Warning",	//状态，多个逗号分隔，不勾选传所有的，Success：0
        "CHECK_STATE":"0,1",	//处理状态，多个逗号分隔，不勾选传所有的
        "PORT_CODES":"asdasdc,qqqqq",	//组合模式，A区勾选的组合代码，多个逗号分隔，必须勾选；指标模式：不勾选传所有组合代码
        "INDEX_CODES":"70049_TEST,80002_TEST_WARN",	//组合模式，B区勾选的指标代码，多个逗号分隔，不勾选传所有指标代码；指标模式：A区，必须勾选
        "SEARCH_MODE":"SEARCH_MODE_INDEX",	//SEARCH_MODE_INDEX：指标模式，SEARCH_MODE_PORT：组合模式
        "SEARCH_STYLE":"SEARCH_STYLE_BUS"	//SEARCH_STYLE_BUS：按业务日期，SEARCH_STYLE_EXEC：按执行日期
    },
    "page":{
        "currPage":1,
        "pageCount":0,
        "totalNum":0,
        "pageSize":100,
        "usePage":true
    },
    "allPortCacheList":[	//刚进页面获取的组合缓存
        {
            "portCode":"777888",
            "portName":"ROY融资融券",
            "datCode":"ASS_ZCGLJH",
            "datCls":"CLS_PT",
            "groupList":[

            ],
            "shortNumList":[

            ]
        }
    ]
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//返回的数据只有子节点的，父节点根据子节点构建
//组合模式根据c_PORT_CODE相同的构建父节点，组合下面挂指标
//指标模式根据c_INDEX_CODE相同的构建父节点，指标下面挂组合
//构建的父节点要根据c_MONITOR_STATE来统计：正常(1)、异常(2)、预警(3)、程序错误(4)、未执行(5)的数量，放到括号中
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "dataList": [
            {
                "id": "",
                "c_IDEN": "5747678706233292546",
                "c_INDEX_CODE": "70049_TEST",
                "c_INDEX_NAME": "70049_TEST",
                "c_MONITOR_STATE": "Warning",	//监控状态，Success=成功，Warning=预警，Fail=异常，Error=程序错误，Pending=未执行
                "c_EXECUTE_STATE": "2",	//执行状态，0=未执行，1=执行中（查询列表不会出现此状态），2=正常执行，3=程序错误
                "c_PORT_CODE": "1t2222",
                "c_PORT_NAME": "1t2222",
                "c_CHECK_STATE": "0",	//处理状态，0=未处理，1=已处理
                "c_UPDATE_TIME": "20210210 14:36:46",	//最近监控时间
                "c_EXE_RESULT": "70049需求测试，失败",	//结果描述
                "c_CHECK_TIME": "20210210 15:15:06",	//确认时间
                "operator": "ht",	//确认人
                "c_COMMENT": "去玩儿",		//确认备注
                "c_MONITOR_DATE": "2021-02-10",	//业务日期
                "c_BIZ_PERIOD": "2021-02-10",
                "c_DAT_CLS": "ASS_QDII",
                "c_DAT_NAME": "QDII证券基金",
                "c_TYPE_CODE": "default",
                "c_TYPE_NAME": "未分类指标",
                "modifier": "ht",	//执行人
                "total": 0,
                "d_EXECUTE_BEGIN": "20210210 14:36:37",
                "executeId": "c3e06e1c-56e9-4d23-b66a-c6cfc2189f19",
                "c_RISK_LEVEL": "high",
                "c_RISK_LEVEL_NAME": "高",
                "c_ISPUBLIC": "0",
                "indexLevel": 0
            },
            {
                "id": "",
                "c_IDEN": "5747678706233292538",
                "c_INDEX_CODE": "70049_TEST",
                "c_INDEX_NAME": "70049_TEST",
                "c_MONITOR_STATE": "Warning",
                "c_EXECUTE_STATE": "2",
                "c_PORT_CODE": "qqqqq",
                "c_PORT_NAME": "qqqqqqqqq",
                "c_CHECK_STATE": "0",
                "c_UPDATE_TIME": "20210210 14:36:42",
```

## B区-查询（获取总记录条数）

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/summary/controller/IMonitorSummaryServiceController/queryByConditionNewCount?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
//和查询的参数基本一样，唯一不同就是少了分页的信息
{
    "paraMap":{
        "dataClass":"MonitorSummary",	//写死
        "MONITOR_START_DATE":"2021-02-10",	//开始日期，如果只显示开始日期，则结束日期等于开始日期
        "MONITOR_END_DATE":"2021-02-10",	//结束日期
        "MONITOR_STATE":"Fail,Warning",	//状态，多个逗号分隔，不勾选传所有的
        "CHECK_STATE":"0,1",	//处理状态，多个逗号分隔，不勾选传所有的
        "PORT_CODES":"asdasdc,qqqqq",	//组合模式，A区勾选的组合代码，多个逗号分隔，必须勾选；指标模式：不勾选传所有组合代码
        "INDEX_CODES":"70049_TEST,80002_TEST_WARN",	//组合模式，B区勾选的指标代码，多个逗号分隔，不勾选传所有指标代码；指标模式：A区，必须勾选
        "SEARCH_MODE":"SEARCH_MODE_INDEX",	//SEARCH_MODE_INDEX：指标模式，SEARCH_MODE_PORT：组合模式
        "SEARCH_STYLE":"SEARCH_STYLE_BUS"	//SEARCH_STYLE_BUS：按业务日期，SEARCH_STYLE_EXEC：按执行日期
    },
    "allPortCacheList":[	//刚进页面获取的组合缓存
        {
            "portCode":"777888",
            "portName":"ROY融资融券",
            "datCode":"ASS_ZCGLJH",
            "datCls":"CLS_PT",
            "groupList":[

            ],
            "shortNumList":[

            ]
        }
    ]
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "401",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 获取参数-B区查询返回的结果按几级树形显示（暂时不做，默认按两级显示）

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/paramConfig/controller/IMonitorSysParamServiceController/getMonitorLogSummaryTreeTabParam?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
(无)
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "TREE_TAB2": " "	//TREE_TAB2：按2级，TREE_TAB3:按3级，3级中又分为，指标树（IndexTree）和风险级别（RiskLevel）
    },
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 执行-重复执行（勾选B区中的记录行，优先判断）

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/controller/IMonitoringExecuteServiceController/reExecute?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "executeId":"a7ba2a73-6f92-43df-af6c-17800c40b24d",	//由前端随机生成的uuid，唯一executeId
    "selectedParams":[	//B区行记录，组合代码##指标代码##监控日期
        "100016##STOCK_JZZZLJC##2021-02-19",
        "100122##STOCK_JZZZLJC##2021-02-19"
    ]
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//返回值不用关心
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 执行-批量执行（勾选A区和B区）

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/controller/IMonitoringExecuteServiceController/executeNonBiz?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
//指标代码和组合代码都必须勾选才能执行
{
    "portCodes":[	//A区或B区勾选的组合代码
        "asdasdc",
        "qqqqq",
        "3rt4234"
    ],
    "indexCodes":[	//A区或B区勾选的指标代码
        "STOCK_JZZZLJC"
    ],
    "strBeginDate":"2021-02-19",	//监控日期
    "strEndDate":"2021-02-19",
    "executeId":"c395666d-2e66-4cae-8911-d42ea5f498c8"	//由前端随机生成的uuid，唯一executeId
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//返回值不用关心
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "",
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 执行-拿进度

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/controller/IMonitoringExecuteServiceController/getProgress1?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "executeId":"c395666d-2e66-4cae-8911-d42ea5f498c8",	//上一步产生的executeId
    "removeDetail":"true",	//写死
    "removeExecuteId":"false"	//写死
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
//此请求会每隔500ms调一次
//total <> 0，且total <= completNum，停止定时器
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "total": 2,	//任务总数
        "completNum": 2	//任务完成数
    },
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 获取保存完成总数量（调一次）

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/controller/IMonitoringExecuteServiceController/getSaveFinishedNum?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
c395666d-2e66-4cae-8911-d42ea5f498c8	//前面生成的executeId
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "2",	//需要保存的总数量
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 获取已经保存完成数量-定时获取

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/controller/IMonitoringExecuteServiceController/getSaveLogTaskNum?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
c395666d-2e66-4cae-8911-d42ea5f498c8	//前面生成的executeId
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": "2",	//每500ms调一次获取已经保存完成的数量，直到此数量等于上面请求的总数量停止
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```

## 执行日志-定时获取

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/summary/controller/IMonitorSummaryServiceController/queryMonitorExcuteLog1?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
Body类型：x-www-form-urlencodeed
参数：executeId=ce80dddb-2727-499e-8038-681a53a35062&maxCount=2000
说明：executeId：前面生成的执行id
	 maxCount：最大返回数量，写死2000
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "id": "",
        "logs": {
            "0": [],	//未执行
            "1": [],	//执行中
            "2": [	//成功
                {
                    "id": "",
                    "monitor": "2021-02-20",
                    "portCode": "111TTAA",
                    "portName": "111TTAA",
                    "state": "2",
                    "reason": "执行监控指标【净值增长率检查】对组合【111TTAA】进行【2021-02-20】日的业务检查正常完成",
                    "executeBegin": "20210222 11:49:24",
                    "executeEnd": "20210222 11:49:25",
                    "excuteid": "ce80dddb-2727-499e-8038-681a53a35062"
                },
                {
                    "id": "",
                    "monitor": "2021-02-20",
                    "portCode": "1212tt",
                    "portName": "子组合2",
                    "state": "2",
                    "reason": "执行监控指标【净值增长率检查】对组合【1212tt】进行【2021-02-20】日的业务检查正常完成",
                    "executeBegin": "20210222 11:49:24",
                    "executeEnd": "20210222 11:49:25",
                    "excuteid": "ce80dddb-2727-499e-8038-681a53a35062"
                }
            ],
            "3": []	//失败
        },
        "counts": {
            "0": "0",
            "1": "0",
            "2": "2",
            "3": "0"
        }
    },
    "message": "",
    "success": true
```

## 执行日志-完成后需要分页

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/summary/controller/IMonitorSummaryServiceController/queryMonitorExcuteLog2?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
Body类型：x-www-form-urlencodeed
参数：executeId=ce80dddb-2727-499e-8038-681a53a35062&state=2&startIndex=1&endIndex=100
说明：executeId：前面生成的执行id
	 state：当前获得活动的tab 执行状态
	 startIndex：每一页起始行
	 endIndex：每一页截止行
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": [
        {
            "id": "",
            "monitor": "2021-02-20",
            "portCode": "111TTAA",

            "executeEnd": "20210222 11:49:25",
            "excuteid": "ce80dddb-2727-499e-8038-681a53a35062"
        },
        {
            "id": "",
            "monitor": "2021-02-20",
            "portCode": "1212tt",
            "portName": "子组合2",
            "state": "2",
            "reason": "执行监控指标【净值增长率检查】对组合【1212tt】进行【2021-02-20】日的业务检查正常完成",
            "executeBegin": "20210222 11:49:24",
            "executeEnd": "20210222 11:49:25",
            "excuteid": "ce80dddb-2727-499e-8038-681a53a35062"
        }
```

```json
        "2020-12-07"
    ],
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```
