## 点击详情-查询一级明细数据

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/monitorLog/controller/IMonitorLogDetailNewServiceController/queryByCondition/page?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "paraMap":{
        "dataClass":"MonitorLogDetailNew",	//写死
        "START_DATE":"2020-12-07",	//总览记录的业务日期
        "END_DATE":"2020-12-07",	//点击详情进来，结束日期和开始日期一样
        "INDEX_CODE":"70049_TEST",	//总览记录的指标代码
        "PORT_CODE":"100122",	//总览记录的组合代码
        "TAB_NAME":"-",	//上面查询到的表名
        "IDEN_RELA":"5747678706233260086",	//总览记录的id
        "MONITOR_STATE":"Warning,Fail",	//监控状态，点击详情进来时传Warning,Fail，即预警和异常，成功:Success
        "ARRAY_DETAIL_STATE":"1,2",	//监控状态，点击详情进来时传1,2，即预警和异常，Success：0
        "CHECK_STATE":"0,1",	//处理状态，点击详情进来时传所有
        "MONITOR_STATE_MAIN":"Warning",	//总览记录的监控状态
        "ARRAY_EXPAND_COL":"C_COL4|Demo测试4,Demo测试20"	//扩展条件，字段|字段值1,字段值2，选择了该条件，参数才传入，否则不传
    },
    "page":{
        "currPage":1,
        "pageCount":0,
        "totalNum":0,
        "pageSize":100,
        "usePage":true
    }
}
```

### 返回值示例


## 点击详情-查询预警的颜色

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/paramConfig/controller/IMonitorSysParamServiceController/getAutoSetColorParam?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
(无)
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": {
        "BackColor": "-16711936"	//BackColor：背景色，ForeColor：前景色，将值转成16进制，就是颜色RGB
    },
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 点击一级明细记录-查询二级明细表名

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/monitorLog/controller/IMonitoringSubDetailServiceController/getTabs?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "IdenRela":"5747678706233260086",	//一级明细记录中的idenRela
    "TabName":"-"	//一级明细记录中的tabName
}
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": [
        "业务流水信息"
    ],
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 点击一级明细记录-查询二级明细数据

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/monitorLog/controller/IMonitoringSubDetailServiceController/queryByCondition/page?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
{
    "paraMap":{
        "dataClass":"MonitoringSubResult",	//写死
        "IdenRela":"5747678706233260086",	//一级记录的idenRela
        "DetailIndex":"2",	//对应一级记录detailIndex
        "MonitorDate":"2020-12-07",	//对应总览记录c_Monitor_Date
        "TabName":"-",	//对应一级记录tabName
        "HeadIndex":"2",	//对应一级记录detailIndex
        "SubTabName":"业务流水信息"	//上面查出来的表名
    },
    "page":{
        "currPage":1,
        "pageCount":0,
        "totalNum":0,
        "pageSize":100,
        "usePage":true
    }
}
```

### 返回值示例


## 总览记录-确认（含批量）

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/summary/controller/IMonitorSummaryServiceController/updateComment?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
Body类型：x-www-form-urlencodeed
参数：c_Iden=5747678706233260086&c_Comment=123&monitorDate=2020-12-07
说明：c_Iden：总览记录的id，多个使用%分隔
	 c_Comment：输入的备注信息
	 monitorDate：总览记录的业务日期c_Monitor_Date
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": true,
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 总览记录-反确认（含批量）

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/summary/controller/IMonitorSummaryServiceController/unConfirmIndexLog?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
Body类型：x-www-form-urlencodeed
参数：c_Iden=5747678706233260086&monitorDate=2020-12-07
说明：c_Iden：总览记录的id，多个使用%分隔
	 monitorDate：总览记录的业务日期c_Monitor_Date
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": true,
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 确认、反确认的局部刷新

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/summary/controller/IMonitorSummaryServiceController/queryMonitorSummaryByIds?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
[
    "5747678706233260086"	//id列表
]
```

### 返回值示例

```json
{
    "code": "success",
    "data": [
        {
            "id": "",
            "c_IDEN": "5747678706233260086",
            "c_CHECK_STATE": "0",
            "c_CHECK_TIME": "20210303 16:55:40",
            "operator": "ht",
            "total": 0
        }
    ],
    "message": "",
    "success": true
}
```



## 一级明细记录-确认（含批量）

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json

    "COMMENT":"1234",	//输入的备注信息
```

## 一级明细记录-反确认（含批量）

### 方法说明

请求URL：/yssmonitor-testor/YSSUCOBRIDGE/ws/com/yss/uco/monitor/support/monitorLog/controller/IMonitorLogDetailNewServiceController/doUnConfirmLogDetailNew?serviceId=yssmonitor-testor

请求方式：POST

### 参数示例

```json
//一级明细记录勾选的json当字符串传入
{
    "DATALIST":"[{"idenRela":"5747678706233260139","tabName":"-","detailIndex":2,"monitorState":"2","bizDate":"","monitorDate":"2021-12-09","monitorDesc":"1234","auditState":"已处理","operUser":"ht","auditDate":"20210303 20:21:57","cellExceptoins":"","dataID":"","exeResult":null,"col1":"2020-12-07","col2":"111TTAA","col3":"111TTAA","col4":"Demo测试6","col5":"","col6":"","col7":"","col8":"","col9":"","col10":"","col11":"","col12":"","col13":"","col14":"","col15":"","col16":"","col17":"","col18":"","col19":"","col20":"","col21":"","col22":"","col23":"","col24":"","col25":"","col26":"","col27":"","col28":"","col29":"","col30":"","col31":"","col32":"","col33":"","col34":"","col35":"","col36":"","col37":"","col38":"","col39":"","col40":"","col41":"","col42":"","col43":"","col44":"","col45":"","col46":"","col47":"","col48":"","col49":"","col50":"","id":"57079811"},{"idenRela":"5747678706233260139","tabName":"-","detailIndex":4,"monitorState":"2","bizDate":"","monitorDate":"2021-12-09","monitorDesc":"1234","auditState":"已处理","operUser":"ht","auditDate":"20210303     "MONITORDATE":"2021-12-09"	//总览的业务日期
}
```

```json
    "code": "success",
    "data": "true",

    "success": true
```
